refer: in BUS8;","                        equal : out BIT);","    end component;","","    component   TRANSMITTER_BOX1 port( eq, ck: in BIT;","                        su, sd: out BIT);","    end component;","","    signal      EQUAL: BIT;","","begin","","SENSOR:         SENSOR_BOX port map( DR_SPEED, CONTROL, REF_SPEED, EQUAL);","TRANSMITTER:    TRANSMITTER_BOX1 port map( EQUAL, CONTROL, FASTER, SLOWER);","","end ACC_BODY;","","--*******************************************************","","--ENTITY SENSOR_BOX","","use buses.all;","","entity SENSOR_BOX is port(pulses, reset: in BIT; refer: in BUS8;","                          equal: out BIT) ;","end SENSOR_BOX;","","architecture SENSOR_BODY of SENSOR_BOX is","     ","        component COUNTER_8 port(pulses,reset: in BIT; c: out BUS8);","	end component;","","        component COMPARATOR_8 port(ina,inb: in BUS8;eql: out BIT);","	end component;","","        signal C: BUS8;","","begin","","COUNTER:        COUNTER_8 port map(pulses,reset,C);","COMPARATOR:     COMPARATOR_8 port map(C,refer,equal);","","end SENSOR_BODY;","","--***********************************************","","-- ENTITY TRANSMITTER_BOX","","entity TRANSMITTER_BOX1 is port( eq, ck: in BIT;
